- Re-export attributes header (`with`‚Üí`{`) ‚Üí Before `with` (block); the after-`}` comment trails past `;` in both ‚Äî [exports/attributes_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/attributes_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Empty `with {}` comment (`with`‚Üí`{`, inside `{}`) ‚Üí Before `with`; the after-`}` comment trails past `;` in both ‚Äî [attributes_empty_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/attributes_empty_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Import-attribute value's leading line comment authored on the `:` line (`with { type: // c‚èé'json' }`) ‚Üí Prettier floats it past the value to trail it (`type: 'json' // c`, dual-stable); tsv keeps it leading the value, breaking after `:` and indenting (an own-line line comment matches ‚Äî plain `attributes_value_comment`; a same-gap block stays inline ‚Äî plain `attributes_comma_comment`) ‚Äî [attributes_value_colon_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/attributes_value_colon_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Import-attribute key‚Üí`:` gap line comment (`with { type // c‚èé: 'json' }`) ‚Üí Prettier floats it past the value to trail it (`type: 'json' // c`); tsv keeps it trailing the key and drops `: value` to a continuation line (`type // c‚èé\t: 'json'`, the uniform forced-continuation indent ‚Äî same as the object-property / type-member key‚Üí`:` line comment; a same-gap block stays inline ‚Äî plain `attributes_comma_comment`) ‚Äî [attributes_key_colon_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/attributes_key_colon_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Own-line line comment before a statement's `;`, blank line after ‚Üí Prettier floats the blank above the comment (promoting it to lead the next statement); tsv keeps the blank below (comment stays with its statement). General ‚Äî imports are the example, the `; // 1` is incidental ‚Äî [source_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/source_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Import keyword/`from`‚Üísource (line) ‚Üí In place flat (bare/empty), into braces (named), after `;` (default); tsv indents ‚Äî [source_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/source_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Re-export `from`‚Üísource (line) ‚Üí In place flat (empty/export-all), into braces (named); tsv indents ‚Äî [source_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/source_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Module header gap, **multiline block** (`import { a } from /* x‚èéy */‚èé'./a'`) ‚Üí The author broke after a comment that cannot be reflowed (inlining would swallow the `*/` line into the header), so the break is forced and tsv indents the continuation one level ‚Äî [¬ßUniform Forced-Continuation Indent](#uniform-forced-continuation-indent), uniformly with the same gap's *line* comment and with every value gap's multiline block (`const x =‚èé\t/* x‚èéy */‚èé\t1;`). The comment's own interior lines stay flush; tsv never re-indents a comment body. Prettier relocates the comment into the braces (imports) or past `from` (export-all) and leaves the continuation flat ‚Äî [imports/header_multiline_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/header_multiline_block_comment_prettier_divergence/), [exports/header_multiline_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/header_multiline_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Module header gap, **own-line block** (`import { a }‚èé/* c */‚èéfrom './a'`) ‚Üí Prettier preserves the break and relocates the comment per gap (into the braces as a specifier-trailing comment for specifiers‚Üí`from`, as a leading comment for keyword‚Üí`{`, flat for default‚Üí`from`); tsv trails it inline and reflows the value onto the header line. A module header is a keyword‚Üívalue gap, so a single-line block collapses from any authored position ‚Äî the shared `comment_hangs_next` rule its `export default` / `export =` siblings use ([¬ßAuthored breaks in value position](#authored-breaks-in-value-position)); an authored blank line in the gap yields with the break. Prettier's first pass is unstable here, so the chain is pinned `prettier_intermediate_to_variant_*` ‚Üí `variant_*` ‚Äî [header_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/header_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- No-`from` empty export keyword‚Üí`{}` (line) ‚Üí In place flat; tsv indents ‚Äî [empty_no_from_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/empty_no_from_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- `export`/`export default`‚Üídeclaration (line) ‚Üí In place flat; tsv indents ‚Äî [export_declaration_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/syntax/comments/export_declaration_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- `export default`‚Üívalue / `export =`‚Üívalue, **same-line** comment + value on the next line ‚Üí comment position matches (both trail the keyword/`=`); prettier preserves the author's line break, tsv **reflows the value inline**. The author's break carries no meaning here ‚Äî a block comment does not run to end-of-line, so nothing forces the tail off the line ‚Äî and tsv's TS printer reflows this gap at every other value position (`const`/`let` `=`, `type =`, class property, object value, parameter default, arrow body, `:` annotation, return type, `satisfies`, `as`). See [¬ßAuthored breaks in value position](#authored-breaks-in-value-position) ‚Äî [default_value_same_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/default_value_same_line_comment_prettier_divergence/), [export_equals_value_same_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/export_equals_value_same_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Declaration keyword‚Üíname (line; `function`/`class`/`enum`/`declare function`) ‚Üí In place flat; tsv indents ‚Äî [keyword_name_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/syntax/comments/keyword_name_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Between `else` and non-block body (line) ‚Üí Prettier keeps it after `else` on its own line (indented); tsv keeps it trailing `else` on the same line ‚Äî [else_line_comment_nonblock](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/if/else_line_comment_nonblock_prettier_divergence/)
- Union infix `\|` line comment ‚Üí Trailing on previous member ‚Äî [union_infix_pipe_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/union_infix_pipe_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Retained paren union member comment ‚Üí A trailing block comment hoisted after `)`; a leading one stays inside ‚Äî [union_intersection_retained_paren_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/union_intersection_retained_paren_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Retained paren union member line cmt ‚Üí Comment stays inside parens (both); tsv keeps inner union inline (union-fit), prettier explodes it one-per-line ‚Äî [union_intersection_retained_paren_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/union_intersection_retained_paren_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Retained paren union leading line cmt ‚Üí Before the 1st member (out of parens); tsv keeps it inside the parens. Covers a paren-union member, a paren-intersection-with-trailing-object member (whose aligned layout is built from the already-unwrapped inner type ‚Äî so the paren's own gap must be threaded in, or the comment is silently dropped), and later paren-function / -conditional / -intersection members (for which prettier trails the comment on the previous member) ‚Äî for every member, not just the first ‚Äî [union_intersection_retained_paren_leading_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/union_intersection_retained_paren_leading_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Redundant paren member leading line cmt ‚Üí tsv leads the member with it on its own line before the `| ` (the parens are stripped, so it can't stay inside); prettier trails it on the previous member (`| a // c`). Dual-stable ‚Äî the stripped-paren counterpart of the retained-paren keep-inside rule; a comment never changes which parens are retained, only where it renders once they are ‚Äî [union_redundant_paren_member_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/union_redundant_paren_member_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Redundant paren member mixed / trailing cmt (union) ‚Üí the mixed / trailing extension of the entry above. A redundant paren shell around a **later** union member holds a leading **line** comment with a **leading block** (mixed, `A | (/* b */ // c‚èé B)`) or a **trailing** comment (`A | (// c‚èé B /* t */)`), and the double-nested forms. tsv renders the run between the `| ` members ‚Äî block and line each on their own line before the member's `| `, a trailing block staying inline after the member (`| A‚èé /* b */‚èé // c‚èé | B`) ‚Äî keeping every comment where the author wrote it, idempotent in one pass (the pass-1 member-hang reflowed otherwise). Prettier floats the leading run to trail the previous member (`| A /* b */ // c`), dual-stable, so it is a `variant_trailing` exactly as the pure-line sibling ‚Äî [union_redundant_paren_member_mixed_trailing_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/union_redundant_paren_member_mixed_trailing_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Redundant paren **first** member mixed / trailing cmt (intersection) ‚Üí the intersection-first-member analog of the union entry above, and the intersection extension of the pure-line [intersection_leading_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/intersection_leading_line_comment_prettier_divergence/) below. A redundant paren shell around the **first** member of an intersection holds a leading **line** comment with a **leading block** (mixed, `(/* b */ // c‚èé A) & B`) or a **trailing** comment (`(// c‚èé A /* t */) & B`), and the double-nested forms. tsv strips the shell and hangs the run at the same fixed point the bare authoring settles on ‚Äî the leading block trails `=` inline, the line comment forces the value onto its own line, a trailing block trails the member inline, and the intersection stays inline (`type T = /* b */‚èé // c‚èé A & B`) ‚Äî the keyword‚Üívalue hang seam (bug188), routed through the first-member hoist. Prettier breaks after `=` and drops the run onto its own line(s). The two cases differ only in prettier's *paren-shell* path: both pass through an unstable member-hang first pass (`A &‚èé B` broken), but the **trailing** case's terminal is the dual-stable own-line form (a `variant_own_line`, `prettier_intermediate_to_variant`) ‚Äî [intersection_redundant_paren_first_member_trailing_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/intersection_redundant_paren_first_member_trailing_line_comment_prettier_divergence/) ‚Äî while the **mixed** case's terminal keeps prettier's `/* b */ // c` *glued* on one line, a form tsv un-glues to its own `output_prettier` ‚Äî a `divergent_variant`, pinned by the `prettier_intermediate_to_divergent_variant_*` marker (rule N7c, the intermediate-convergence family's `divergent_variant` target) ‚Äî [intersection_redundant_paren_first_member_mixed_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/intersection_redundant_paren_first_member_mixed_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Retained paren member **own-line leading** line cmt (collapsing intersection) ‚Üí Out of parens, onto its own line before `(`, intersection broken; tsv keeps it inside the parens, forcing the member to break open ‚Äî [union_intersection_paren_member_own_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/union_intersection_paren_member_own_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Retained paren intersection member cmt ‚Üí Outside the parens (after `)`/`(`) ‚Äî [retained_paren_intersection_member_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/retained_paren_intersection_member_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Type alias head to `=` (line) ‚Üí After `=` (right of operator); when the value is a break-forced non-hugging union, `=` drops onto its own line and members hang at the `=` level (not one deeper) ‚Äî [type_alias_line_pre_equals](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/type_alias_line_pre_equals_prettier_divergence/), [type_alias_line_pre_equals_break](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/type_alias_line_pre_equals_break_prettier_divergence/)
- Type param keyword to value (own-line) ‚Üí Up onto the keyword line ‚Äî [type_param_keyword_own_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/type_param_keyword_own_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Function param default to value (line) ‚Üí Floated out to trail the whole parameter (after the value) ‚Äî [param_default_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/function/param_default_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Name/key to default `=` (line) ‚Üí Floated out to trail the whole binding (after the value); the *before*-`=` counterpart of the row above, at a parameter default and every destructuring default (object/array/param binding). tsv keeps it trailing the name with `= value` on the next line (a `//` there would otherwise swallow the `=`) ‚Äî [default_equals_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/destructuring/default_equals_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- `as`/`satisfies` keyword to type (line) ‚Üí Statement-trailing (after `;`) ‚Äî [as_satisfies_value_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_satisfies_value_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- **Redundant paren shell at a keyword‚Üívalue hang, mixed / trailing comment** ‚Üí the mixed / trailing extension of the pure-line seam above. A redundant paren shell around the value of a keyword‚Üívalue hang site whose leading gap holds a **block before the line comment** (mixed, `(/* b */ // c‚èé X)`), or whose trailing gap holds a **comment after the value** (trailing, `(// c‚èé X /* t */)`), and the double-nested `((‚Ä¶))` forms. tsv strips the shell and hangs the whole run at the same fixed point the bare (paren-free) authoring settles on ‚Äî the leading block trails the keyword inline, the line comment forces the value onto its own line, and the trailing comment trails the value (a cast, being a value position, defers a trailing block past the statement `;` via `line_suffix`; type positions keep it inline). Prettier floats or reorders the comments per site. Across every hang site: the `as`/`satisfies` cast ‚Äî [as_satisfies_value_mixed_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_satisfies_value_mixed_comment_prettier_divergence/), [as_satisfies_value_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_satisfies_value_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/) ‚Äî the prefix type-operator (`keyof`/`typeof`/`readonly`) ‚Äî [type_operator_keyword_mixed_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_operator_keyword_mixed_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/) ‚Äî the type-predicate `is` ‚Äî [predicate_is_mixed_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/predicate_is_mixed_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/) ‚Äî the mapped-type value ‚Äî [mapped_value_mixed_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/mapped_value_mixed_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/) ‚Äî the `: T` annotation ‚Äî [annotation_mixed_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/annotation_mixed_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/) ‚Äî the type-parameter `= default` / `extends` constraint ‚Äî [constraint_default_mixed_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_params/constraint_default_mixed_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/) ‚Äî and the type-alias `= T` RHS (its own `build_type_alias_eq_value_doc`, routed through the same seam) ‚Äî [type_alias_rhs_mixed_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/type_alias_rhs_mixed_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- **Redundant paren shell trailing block at a value-position cast, no line comment** ‚Üí the no-line-comment sibling of the hang entry above, and a distinct mechanism (bug188's line-comment seam never fires). A redundant paren shell around an `as`/`satisfies` cast type whose trailing gap holds a **block** comment with **no leading line comment** (`(Z /* t */)`, `(/* b */ Z /* t */)`, and the double-nested forms). Because a cast is a **value** position, tsv strips the shell and defers the trailing block past the statement `;` (via `line_suffix`) ‚Äî a leading block trails the keyword inline ‚Äî reaching `x as Z; /* t */` in one pass where prettier takes two (prettier is non-idempotent on the shell but converges to the same fixed point, so the shells are `unformatted_ours` + `prettier_intermediate`, not an end-state divergence). Only the two value-position casts need this; every type position (`keyof`, mapped, `: T`, `is`, type-param, conditional `extends`, union/intersection member) keeps a trailing block inline and is already idempotent ‚Äî [as_satisfies_value_trailing_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_satisfies_value_trailing_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- `as const` keyword to `const` ‚Üí A block comment moves before the whole expression (`1 /* c */ as const`); a line comment floats past the statement (`1 as const; // c`). tsv keeps either between `as` and `const` (`1 as /* c */ const`; the line comment trails the keyword with `const` on the next line), matching the regular `as <type>` case that both formatters preserve. Unique to the `const` assertion ‚Äî `as <type>`, `as <literal>`, and `satisfies const` all stay put in both ‚Äî [as_const_keyword_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_const_keyword_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Angle-bracket type assertion, trailing `<` / trailing `>` (line) ‚Üí trailing-`<` onto its own line; trailing-`>` into the cast, trailing the type (`<string> // c` ‚Üí `<‚èéstring // c‚èé>z`, tsv keeps it after `>` leading the expression one indent in). Own-line-after-`<` and trailing-the-type break the cast in both formatters and match ‚Äî [type_assertion_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_assertion_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Angle-bracket type assertion, own-line before `>` after a trailing-type comment (line) ‚Üí No fixed point (prettier oscillates the comment across `>`); tsv keeps it on its own line before `>` inside the cast ‚Äî [type_assertion_close_own_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_assertion_close_own_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Angle-bracket type assertion, own-line after `>` before the expression (line) ‚Üí Into the cast trailing the type, over two passes (pass 1 glues it onto `>`, pass 2 moves it inside ‚Äî F4 audit signature); tsv keeps it on its own line leading the expression ‚Äî [type_assertion_expr_own_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_assertion_expr_own_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Angle-bracket type assertion robustness (object operand after `>`; block+line trailing `<`) ‚Üí operand-after-`>` comment relocated into the cast, trailing-`<` block+line moved to their own line; tsv preserves each. A generic cast type with a nested `>` matches prettier (the close `>` is found past the type's own) ‚Äî [type_assertion_line_comment_robustness](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_assertion_line_comment_robustness_prettier_divergence/)
- Heritage keyword to type (line) ‚Üí Up before the keyword ‚Äî [extends_keyword_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/class/extends_keyword_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Heritage list, line comments across elements ‚Üí first element's leading comment Up before the keyword; tsv keeps each comment where written (leading first element after the keyword, per-element trailing/leading intact). When a keyword‚Üífirst-element line comment forced the items onto their own lines, the list was joined with a plain `", "`, so a per-element line comment swallowed the next element (`// c1, B` ‚Äî non-reparseable content loss); the list now joins comma-baking-aware. `extends` and `implements` alike ‚Äî [heritage_element_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/class/heritage_element_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)

See the keyword‚Üívalue block-comment collapse rule below ‚Äî [heritage_keyword_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/class/heritage_keyword_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Conditional `extends` to check (line) ‚Üí Trailing the extends-type ‚Äî [check_extends_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/conditional/check_extends_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Conditional `extends` redundant paren shell, mixed / trailing cmt ‚Üí a redundant paren shell around the `extends`-type whose leading gap holds a **line** comment alongside a **leading block** (mixed, `(/* b */ // c‚èé B)`) or a **trailing** comment (`(// c‚èé B /* t */)`), and the double-nested forms. tsv strips the shell and **hangs** the run at the same fixed point the bare authoring settles on (`A extends /* b */ // c‚èé B` / `A extends // c‚èé B /* t */`) ‚Äî the leading block trails `extends` inline, the line comment forces the extends-type onto its own line, a trailing block trails it inline. The **pure-line** shell keeps its own trail-on-inner canonical (`A extends B // c`, the non-divergence [extends_paren_leading_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/conditional/extends_paren_leading_line_comment/)); only mixed/trailing hang, because trailing a leading block would move it leading‚Üítrailing and the trailing case would reorder (a `//` must end its line). - Intersection member trailing line cmt, member glued to a following member ‚Üí `lineSuffix`-relocated past the object-adjacency-glued members to the end of the visual line ‚Äî across a member boundary (`{ c } // c‚èé& D` ‚Üí trails `D`), and past `;` (`B // c‚èé& { c }` ‚Üí trails the whole type, which then collapses inline); tsv keeps it on its member's line and breaks that boundary, gluing the object-adjacent members before it. - Call arg after-comma block + same-line line comment ‚Üí Block relocated before the comma (tsv keeps it on the comma line) ‚Äî [plain](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/nonlast_arg_after_comma_block_then_line_prettier_divergence/), [new](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/new_nonlast_arg_after_comma_block_then_line_prettier_divergence/), [joined](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/multiline_arg_nonlast_after_comma_block_then_line_prettier_divergence/), [chain](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/chained/nonlast_arg_after_comma_block_then_line_prettier_divergence/), [import](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/import_inter_arg_block_then_line_prettier_divergence/)
- Call arg after-comma block, **stranded** (newline before the next arg) ‚Üí Block relocated before the comma (tsv respects the newline and keeps the stranded block on the comma line). A block instead **hugging** the next arg leads it (`C`) and both formatters agree (plain match) ‚Äî [stranded](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/nonlast_arg_after_comma_block_stranded_prettier_divergence/), [import](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/import_inter_arg_stranded_prettier_divergence/) (dynamic `import()` source‚Üíoptions gap; hugging match at [import_inter_arg_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/import_inter_arg_comment/))
- Comma-separated-item after-comma block, **stranded** (newline before the next item) ‚Üí Block relocated before the comma; tsv keeps the stranded block on the comma line (`a, /* c */‚èé b`), a before-comma and a stranded after-comma block in the same gap each preserved independently. One rule (`is_stranded_after_comma_block`) across every comma-separated site: a block **hugging** the next item leads it (both formatters agree); a **stranded** block stays trailing the comma. The stranded block is a **stable** form only when the items sit on separate lines: the multi-declarator statement always breaks its declarators, while the for-init, heritage (`extends`/`implements`), and function-parameter-list gaps collapse to one line when they fit (there the block hugs the next item and both agree) and diverge the same way only once the items wrap. The regular heritage [interface](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/interface/heritage_item_after_comma_block/) / [class](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/class/heritage/heritage_item_after_comma_block/) fixtures pin the hugging case (leads the next item, matching prettier). Function-parameter lists trail the comma like every other site (function declarations, methods, arrows, constructors, Svelte `{#snippet}` params, plus function/constructor **types** via their separate printer). Stranded fixtures: [declarator](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/variable/multiple/after_comma_block_stranded_prettier_divergence/), [for-init](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/for/init_after_comma_block_stranded_prettier_divergence/), heritage [interface](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/interface/heritage_item_after_comma_block_stranded_prettier_divergence/) / [class](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/class/heritage/heritage_item_after_comma_block_stranded_prettier_divergence/), function-param [param](../tests/fixtures/typescript/syntax/comments/param_after_comma_block_stranded_prettier_divergence/), function/constructor-type [param](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/function_type/param_after_comma_block_stranded_prettier_divergence/)
- Call open paren `(` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [open_paren_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/open_paren_comment_prettier_divergence/), [chain](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/chain_open_paren_comment_prettier_divergence/), [new](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/new_open_paren_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Object literal `{` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [open_brace_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/objects/open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Array literal `[` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [open_bracket_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/arrays/open_bracket_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Block body `{` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [block_open_brace_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/block_open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Type-parameter `<` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [open_angle_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_params/open_angle_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Function/constructor-type `(` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [open_paren_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/function_type/open_paren_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Fn/ctor-type pre-arrow `)` trailing (params) ‚Üí Onto the last param (`a: T // c`) ‚Äî [pre_arrow_param_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/function_type/pre_arrow_param_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Fn/method/signature `)`‚Üíreturn-type-`:` line comment ‚Üí Onto the last param (`a: T // c`), params broken; tsv keeps it trailing `)` with `:` forced onto the next line (the `)`‚Üí`=>` counterpart above ‚Äî a `//` there would otherwise swallow the return type). The signature builders hug the single param (it stays flat); arrows, excluded from that hug, break it ‚Äî [return_type_close_paren_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/function/return_type_close_paren_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Fn/method/signature `)`‚Üíreturn-type-`:` **own-line block** comment ‚Üí tsv collapses it inline (`f(a) /* c */ : T`), the same collapse every keyword‚Üívalue gap and the `)`‚Üí`=>` gap apply; prettier relocates it into the parameter list over two passes (`f(a /* c */): T`, a dual-stable `variant_*`). The collapsed inline form is dual-stable too ‚Äî [return_type_close_paren_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/function/return_type_close_paren_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Call/construct signature `(` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line (method keeps) ‚Äî [signature_params_leading_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/signature_params_leading_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Object destructuring `{` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [object_open_brace_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/destructuring/object_open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Array destructuring `[` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [array_open_bracket_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/destructuring/array_open_bracket_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Namespace/module body `{` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [open_brace_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/namespace/open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Class/interface/enum body `{` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [class](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/class/open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/), [interface](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/interface/open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/), [enum](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/enum/open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Type literal body `{` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [type_literal_open_brace_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_literal_open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Import/export specifier `{` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [imports](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/), [exports](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/open_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Tuple type `[` trailing ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [open_bracket_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/tuple/open_bracket_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Index signature `[` trailing (line) ‚Üí Onto its own line (key's leading comment) ‚Äî [index_signature_open_bracket_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_members/index_signature_open_bracket_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Index signature before `]` (own-line line) ‚Üí After `]` (value `:` to next line) ‚Äî [index_signature_close_bracket_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_members/index_signature_close_bracket_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Index signature `]`‚Üívalue-`:` (line) ‚Üí Into brackets, trailing key type ‚Äî [index_signature_bracket_colon_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_members/index_signature_bracket_colon_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Index signature `]`‚Üívalue-`:` (‚â•2 line comments) ‚Üí No fixed point (prettier oscillates); tsv keeps each on its own line ‚Äî [index_signature_bracket_colon_multi_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_members/index_signature_bracket_colon_multi_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Index signature value-`:`‚Üítype under a `]`‚Üí`:` comment (line) ‚Üí Type kept flush (tsv indents continuation) ‚Äî [index_signature_bracket_colon_value_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_members/index_signature_bracket_colon_value_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Index signature in-bracket line comments, **class** context (four positions) ‚Üí `[`/`:`‚Üítype/own-line-before-`]` relocate or stay flush, key‚Üí`:` matches ‚Äî [index_signature_bracket_line_comment_positions](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/class/index_signature_bracket_line_comment_positions_prettier_divergence/)
- Type-argument `<` trailing (multi) ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [type_argument_open_angle_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_argument_open_angle_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Call/`new`-expr type-arg `<` trailing (multi) ‚Üí Onto its own line ‚Äî [type_args_open_angle_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/calls/type_args_open_angle_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Computed-key `[` trailing (line) ‚Üí Out of the brackets to the member's leading line ‚Äî [computed_key_open_bracket_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/objects/computed_key_open_bracket_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Computed-key `[` trailing (line, class) ‚Üí Kept on `[` line, key glued flush ‚Äî [computed_key_open_bracket_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/class/computed_key_open_bracket_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)
- Computed-key key‚Üí`]` (line) ‚Üí Out of the brackets (same-line ‚Üí member's leading line, own-line ‚Üí past `]:` onto the value) ‚Äî [computed_key_close_bracket_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/objects/computed_key_close_bracket_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)

**Prefix type-operator operand hang** (`type A = keyof // c\n\t\tB`). A line comment in a prefix operator's (`keyof`/`typeof`) keyword‚Üíoperand gap, the operand on a later line, has two authorings with two divergence characters. **Trailing** the operator (layout, *not* a relocation): both formatters keep the comment after the operator _and_ the operator on the `=` line, differing only on the operand's indent ‚Äî tsv hangs it one level under the operator (the uniform keyword‚Üívalue layout `append_keyword_value_line_comments`, shared with the type keyword‚Üítype sites in the table above), while Prettier leaves it flush. On its **own line** (relocation + indent): tsv keeps the comment where the author wrote it and hangs the operand below; Prettier pulls the comment *up* onto the operator line and leaves the operand flush ‚Äî the same up-pull it applies to an own-line type-parameter keyword comment and to `infer`. A long _comment-free_ `keyof`/`typeof` still breaks after `=` in both formatters; the comment is what keeps the operator on the `=` line. Content-preserved and idempotent ([type_operator_keyword_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_operator_keyword_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)).

**How tsv treats keyword‚Üívalue block comments** (the gap between a keyword/operator and its **single operand** ‚Äî `as`/`satisfies`, heritage/conditional `extends`, `keyof`/`typeof`/`readonly`, `infer`, a type parameter's `extends`/`=`, predicate `is`, and indexed access `[`‚Üíindex). These are **single-slot gaps**: one keyword/bracket, one operand, no delimited list. The governing principle across the whole comment story is *per construct, emit the least-divergent output that is lossless, idempotent, **and** position-preserving*; at a single-slot gap that lands on **collapse** ‚Äî a block comment collapses to the inline form (`kw /* c */ operand`) whenever it *can* inline losslessly: a **single-line** block in any position (glued, trailing the keyword, or own-line), and a **glued** multiline block, one whose operand already shares the comment's closing line (`kw /* ‚Ä¶‚èé‚Ä¶ */ operand`, the way Prettier keeps it ‚Äî [keyword_value_glued_multiline_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/keyword_value_glued_multiline_block_comment/)). The own-line placement of such a block carries no signal the inline form drops, so tsv keeps the comment after the keyword and collapses. Only a **line** comment (a `//` would swallow the operand) or an **own-line** multiline block (`kw‚èé/* ‚Ä¶‚èé‚Ä¶ */‚èéoperand` ‚Äî inlining it would reflow the author's break) still hangs the operand on its own line, and there tsv keeps the comment where the author wrote it rather than pulling it onto the keyword line ([type_operator_keyword_own_line_multiline_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_operator_keyword_own_line_multiline_block_comment_prettier_divergence/) for the operator family, [indexed_access_own_line_multiline_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/indexed_access_own_line_multiline_block_comment_prettier_divergence/) for the index slot; a template-literal interpolation hangs its type too, but keys the comment‚Äôs own placement on the authoring ‚Äî see the template-literal note below). The gate is `comments_force_own_line_between` (hang iff a line comment, or a multiline block with a newline after it), shared with the type-alias `=` layout ‚Äî whose `=` stays on its line for a glued multiline value too, rather than breaking on the comment's interior newline.

**One question, one predicate.** The hang rule is stated once, as `Printer::comment_hangs_next` (a line comment, or a multiline block with a newline after it), and *both* the gate above and the emitter that gate selects (`build_trailing_comments_hang_next`) ask it ‚Äî so a gate and its emitter cannot answer differently. This matters more than it looks: an emitter keyed on `is_block` alone reads as plausible code, yet it collapses the own-line multiline case its own gate had just flagged as hanging. The layout then rests on an authored newline that the collapse itself destroys, so the format stops being idempotent on its own output ‚Äî the `=` breaks on pass 1 and hugs on pass 2. The rule's two flush-form gaps (indexed access, template-literal interpolation) sat on exactly that split.

Collapse is not a universal law over "single-line block in a bracket" ‚Äî it's the outcome of that principle *at a single-slot gap*. A delimited `<‚Ä¶>` list is a different construct and takes a different outcome (see the list contrast below). Within the gaps, the divergence lives entirely in the **own-line authoring** (`kw‚èé/* c */‚èéoperand`), which the two formatters normalize to different fixed points ‚Äî each fixture's `unformatted_ours_own_line` variant pins tsv's collapse. The two flavors of Prettier fixed point:

- **In-place-collapse gaps.** Prefix type operators `keyof`/`typeof`/`readonly` ([type_operator_keyword_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_operator_keyword_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)) and `infer` ([keyword_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/infer/keyword_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/), line form [keyword_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/infer/keyword_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)): Prettier reaches the *same* inline form, but is **non-idempotent** ‚Äî its first pass pulls the comment onto the keyword line yet leaves the operand on the next line, collapsing fully only on a second pass.
- **Relocation gaps.** `as`/`satisfies` ([as_satisfies_value_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_satisfies_value_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)), type predicate `is` ([predicate_is_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/predicate_is_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)), a type parameter's `extends`/`=` ([constraint_default_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_params/constraint_default_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)), a conditional type's `extends` ([extends_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/conditional/extends_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)), and indexed access `[`‚Üíindex ([indexed_access_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/indexed_access_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)): Prettier collapses *and relocates* the comment across the keyword/bracket (`x /* c */ as A`, `A /* c */[K]`), and reaches that relocation **non-idempotently** in every case ‚Äî its first pass leaves the comment after the keyword and hangs the operand (`x as /* c */‚èéA`, `A[/* c */‚èéK]`), only its second pass moves the comment across (`x /* c */ as A`, `A /* c */[K]`). tsv keeps it after the keyword and collapses in one pass ‚Äî the pure [comment-position](#comment-position-philosophy) divergence. Each fixture pins Prettier's two-pass chain with a `prettier_intermediate_to_variant_own_line` (its unstable first pass) plus a `variant_own_line` (its relocated fixed point, dual-stable in both formatters).
- **Pass-count gaps (same fixed point).** `await`‚Üíoperand and `new`‚Üícallee ([await_new_operand_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/await_new_operand_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)): unlike the relocation gaps above, prettier does **not** move the comment ‚Äî it reaches the *same* fixed point tsv does (`await /* a */ foo`, `new /* b */ Foo()`), just **non-idempotently**. Its first pass pulls the comment up to the keyword while keeping the author's break (`await /* a */‚èéfoo;`), and only its second pass collapses that. tsv collapses in one pass, the same keyword‚Üívalue rule (`comment_hangs_next`) its `as`/`satisfies`, `export =`, and module-header siblings follow. The intermediate form is the bug the fixture guards ‚Äî it *is* the glued authoring with the break kept, so emitting it is not idempotent on its own output. Pinned by a `prettier_intermediate_own_line` (converging to input, not to a `variant_*`, since the fixed points agree).
- **Heritage `extends`/`implements`** ([heritage_keyword_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/class/heritage_keyword_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)): also a relocation gap, but Prettier does **not** collapse it. From the own-line authoring it settles ‚Äî in one pass, stably ‚Äî on the comment on its **own line before** the keyword (`class P‚èé/* c */‚èéextends Q`), never inlining it. tsv collapses to `class P extends /* c */ Q` (after the keyword, inline). So both move the comment relative to the author's break, but Prettier keeps the break while tsv removes it. Prettier's stable form is *not* dual-stable ‚Äî tsv re-collapses it to a *third* form (`class P /* c */ extends Q`) ‚Äî so it is pinned as a `divergent_variant_*` form rather than a `variant_*` (see the note below).

The own-line authoring of a *single-line* block is the only place these gaps diverge; the inline canonical (`kw /* c */ operand`) is dual-stable in both formatters. Only a **line** comment (a `//` can't be inlined ‚Äî it would swallow the operand) or an **own-line multiline** block comment still hangs the operand on its own line; the collapse applies to single-line blocks (any authoring) and glued multiline blocks. The companion **line**-comment divergences (where the hang is forced) are cataloged alongside each gap above.

**List contrast ‚Äî why `<‚Ä¶>` does not collapse.** A delimited type-argument list `<‚Ä¶>` is *not* a single-slot gap, so it takes the other outcome of the same principle: Prettier has a clean, idempotent list-break rule (an own-line comment on an argument breaks the whole `<‚Ä¶>`), and matching it is the least-divergent lossless choice ‚Äî so tsv matches instead of collapsing. A single-argument own-line *block* comment therefore **expands** (`Foo<‚èé/* c */‚èéT‚èé>`, dual-stable in both formatters ‚Äî [single_arg_own_line_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/type_args/single_arg_own_line_block_comment/)) rather than collapsing to `Foo</* c */ T>`; the single-argument case is just the N=1 form of the list and follows the list, not the gap. (A single-argument leading *line* comment hugs `<`/`>` ‚Äî a separate divergence, cataloged under the [open-delimiter trailing](#comment-relocation) entry.) The surface split ‚Äî index `[K]` collapses, `<T>` expands ‚Äî is not an inconsistency: it is the same "diverge only when Prettier is worse" rule landing on *collapse* where Prettier relocates non-idempotently (the index slot) and on *match* where Prettier is already fine (the list).

Two carve-outs keep the operand break instead of collapsing: **`export default`** still hangs (it's the one construct where Prettier *keeps* the operand break, so hanging ‚Äî both broken, tsv indented ‚Äî is the closer indent-only divergence) and **binary/logical operands** (the expression side, where tsv's own-line layout already matches Prettier). The **conditional `?`/`:` branches** (expression ternary and conditional type alike) collapse the single-line own-line form and keep the glued forms glued ‚Äî including a **glued** multiline block (`? /* ‚Ä¶‚èé‚Ä¶ */ A`) ‚Äî and match Prettier there (no divergence fixture). A branch-gap comment the author broke *after* (`: /* c */‚èéB`) keeps that break as a collapsible line: it holds while the conditional is broken and yields when the whole conditional fits, Prettier's own `printLeadingComment` separator and its fixed point ([ternary/operator_block_comment_break](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/ternary/operator_block_comment_break/), [conditional/branch_block_comment_break](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/conditional/branch_block_comment_break/)). One glued-multiline layout gap remains, unrelated to the block-comment gate: a class/interface **heritage** clause keeps a glued multiline inline (`class P extends /* ‚Ä¶‚èé‚Ä¶ */ Q`) where Prettier breaks before the keyword. It lives in its own layout code (the heritage clause), not in `comments_force_own_line_between`.

**Pinning Prettier's fixed point (fixture mechanics).** Because each inline `input` is dual-stable, these fixtures have no `output_prettier` ‚Äî the divergence lives only in the `unformatted_ours_own_line` variant (tsv normalizes it to `input`; Prettier does not). To assert Prettier's actual output on that variant, the in-place-collapse gaps carry a `prettier_intermediate_own_line` (Prettier's unstable first pass, which reconverges to `input`), and the relocation gaps carry a `prettier_intermediate_to_variant_own_line` + a `variant_own_line` (its relocated fixed point, genuinely dual-stable). **Heritage is the exception:** Prettier's fixed point (`class P‚èé/* c */‚èéextends Q`) is Prettier-stable but tsv re-collapses it to a *third* form (`class P /* c */ extends Q`) ‚Äî neither `input` nor Prettier's form. A `variant_*` is meant to be dual-stable (both formatters keep it verbatim), and a `prettier_variant_*` is a Prettier-stable form tsv normalizes to `input`; heritage is neither, so it is pinned by a `divergent_variant_own_line` ‚Äî a `divergent_variant_*` form.

**The `divergent_variant_*` type.** "Prettier keeps `V`, tsv rewrites `V` to a third stable form" is a small recurring category (three distinct stable forms: `input`, Prettier's `V`, and tsv's `ours(V)`). It is pinned by a `divergent_variant_*` fixture file, which asserts `prettier(V) == V`, `ours(V) != input`, `ours(V) != V`, and `ours(ours(V)) == ours(V)` (the third form is itself a fixed point). Besides heritage the category includes the non-block `else` body ([else_line_comment_nonblock](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/if/else_line_comment_nonblock_prettier_divergence/), `divergent_variant_nonblock`) and the blank-inside-relocated-condition form ([do_while/line_before_while_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/do_while/line_before_while_comment_prettier_divergence/), `divergent_variant_spaces` ‚Äî Prettier relocates a `}`‚Üí`while` comment into the condition parens and keeps a blank there; tsv drops it). This is distinct from `variant_*`, whose check requires true dual-stability (`ours(V) == V`), not merely that tsv reaches *a* fixed point from the form.

**No blank above a body block's `{`**: tsv drops an authored blank line before a body-leading own-line comment in the **header `)`‚Üíbody** gap ‚Äî `while (a)‚èé‚èé// c‚èé{` ‚Üí `while (a)‚èé// c‚èé{`, across `if`/`while`/`for` ‚Äî so a body block's `{` never sits below a blank. This is consistent with tsv's own handling when `{` is on the header line (`while (a) {‚èé‚èé// c` also collapses), and Prettier drops it here too, so tsv matches. The residual divergence in this gap is a blank *after* the comment, before `{` (`while (a)‚èé// c‚èé‚èé{`), which Prettier keeps and tsv normalizes, pinned as `prettier_variant_spaces` in [while/line_before_body_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/while/line_before_body_comment_prettier_divergence/).

**The `}`‚Üícontinuation-keyword gap keeps the blank**, and is a different question that merely shares an emitter. There is no body `{` to sit below the blank: it separates two branches of a chain (`}‚èé‚èé// c‚èéelse`, `}‚èé‚èé// c‚èécatch (e) {`, `}‚èé‚èé// c‚èéwhile (a);`), which is real authoring intent, so tsv preserves it. The gap covers `else`, `catch`, `finally`, and a do-while's `while` ‚Äî every keyword that continues a construct across a `}`. Prettier agrees at `else` ([else_blank_before_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/if/else_blank_before_comment/)). At `catch`/`finally` and at a do-while's `while` Prettier is no oracle ‚Äî it relocates the comment away (into the following block's body, or into the condition parens; see the `divergent_variant_*` note above), discarding the blank with it ‚Äî so tsv's own preservation stance governs there ([try/catch_between_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/try/catch_between_comment_prettier_divergence/), [do_while/line_before_while_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/do_while/line_before_while_comment_prettier_divergence/)). The comment's *position* is unchanged in every case ‚Äî only the blank differs.

**A blank line BETWEEN two own-line comments is always preserved**, in every gap ‚Äî this is a separate question from the blank *above* the first comment, which the two entries above split by gap. An authored blank between two comments separates two distinct remarks, exactly as a blank between two statements does, so tsv keeps it in statement lists, class bodies ([syntax/comments/consecutive_blank_lines](../tests/fixtures/typescript/syntax/comments/consecutive_blank_lines/)), object literals, array elements, parameter lists, the header‚Üíbody gap for **both** block and non-block bodies across `if`/`while`/`for`/for-in/for-of ([syntax/comments/between_head_and_body](../tests/fixtures/typescript/syntax/comments/between_head_and_body/)) and `try`/`catch`/`finally` ([try/keyword_body_blank_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/try/keyword_body_blank_comment_prettier_divergence/)), and the `}`‚Üícontinuation-keyword gaps. Prettier agrees in all of them but **one**: it collapses the blank in the `}`‚Üí`else` / `}`‚Üí`else if` gap ‚Äî for line comments, block comments, and every blank in a longer run alike ‚Äî [if/else_blank_between_comments](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/if/else_blank_between_comments_prettier_divergence/). The divergence is Prettier's own inconsistency rather than a tsv stance: where it *relocates* these comments (into the `catch` body, into a do-while's condition parens) it carries the blank along with them, so it treats the blank as meaningful everywhere except the one gap it prints through a different path. Prettier's collapsed form is dual-stable under tsv (that fixture's `variant_collapsed`), so an already-prettier-formatted file does not churn.

**Type-construct gap line comments** (swallow prevention): a line comment in a type construct's delimiter/keyword/operator gap is kept where the author wrote it, the following token dropped to the next line so the `//` cannot swallow it (the shared `build_trailing_comments_hang_next` / `build_leading_comments_break_for_line`). Prettier relocates each differently ‚Äî out to a statement-trailing position, into/after the enclosing brackets, or trailing the source. tsv preserves the authored position uniformly. Emitting the comment inline (the previous behavior at these sites) let the `//` run to end-of-line and absorb the following token ‚Äî non-idempotent **content loss**. Covered: indexed access [indexed_access_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/indexed_access_line_comment_prettier_divergence/), mapped `in`/`as` [mapped/keyword_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/mapped/keyword_line_comment_prettier_divergence/), import-type qualifier [import_type_qualifier_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/import_type_qualifier_line_comment_prettier_divergence/), and tuple rest / named / optional members [tuple/member_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/tuple/member_line_comment_prettier_divergence/). (`infer` lands a break too but takes the indented keyword‚Üívalue hang rather than this flush form, so it diverges ‚Äî see the Infer keyword entry above.)

**A template-literal interpolation is authoring-dependent ‚Äî the one gap that preserves *both* authorings.** The `${`‚Üítype gap takes neither of the forms above wholesale; it keys on where the author put the comment, and each form is a stable fixed point:

- authored **trailing** `${` ‚Üí stays trailing, type below it (`` `a${// c‚èé‚á•B‚èé}` ``). Prettier expands instead, moving the comment down ‚Äî the divergence ([template_literal_interp_trailing_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/template_literal_interp_trailing_comment_prettier_divergence/), width case [template_literal_interp_trailing_comment_long](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/template_literal_interp_trailing_comment_long_prettier_divergence/), where Prettier additionally emits a blank line after `${`). Prettier's expanded output is itself a tsv fixed point (pinned as that fixture's `variant_expanded`), so tsv never pulls the comment back up ‚Äî the two authorings hold two stable forms rather than one collapsing into the other.
- authored **own-line** ‚Üí the interpolation **expands**, the comment keeps its line (`` `a${‚èé// c‚èéB‚èé}` ``). This is prettier's layout, so tsv matches ‚Äî no divergence ([template_literal_interp_own_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/template_literal_interp_own_line_comment/)).

The two questions are independent and keyed on opposite sides of the comment: what *follows* it decides whether the type hangs at all (`comment_hangs_next`, the newline after), what *precedes* it decides whether the comment keeps its own line (the newline before). A glued single-line block still collapses inline (`` `a${/* c */ B}` ``). Both broken forms put `}` on its own line, as a width-driven break does ‚Äî a hanging comment is the *only* break mechanism in play, so a too-wide type simply breaks *inside* the already-broken interpolation instead of a second break firing on top of it.

Why authoring-dependent here, when most gaps pick one canonical form: a single form **cannot** preserve both authorings ‚Äî forcing the expansion moves a trailing-authored comment down (Prettier's choice), forcing the flush form pulls an own-line-authored one up. Both authorings render identically and each form is stable, so there is no lossless-or-idempotent reason to collapse them; the authored break is simply signal, and tsv keeps it. This is the same distinction the type-alias `=` gap already draws (`type A = /* c */ B` hugs, `type A =‚èé/* c */‚èéB` keeps its own line), and it makes the divergence *minimal* ‚Äî only the trailing authoring differs from Prettier.

The `=` keeps the backtick on its line for both (`value_owns_its_comment_break`), since either layout already breaks the template itself.

**Else line comment with non-block body**: `} else // c\nexpr;` ‚Üí Prettier keeps the comment after `else` but drops it onto its own line, indented with the body (`} else\n\t// c\n\texpr;`); tsv keeps it trailing `else` on the same line (`} else // c\n\texpr;`). Affects block consequent, comments-path, and non-block consequent cases. The comment-before-`else` form `} // c\nelse expr;` is also prettier-stable: dual-stable (`variant_comment_before_else`) for the block/comments-path cases, but a `divergent_variant_*` form (`divergent_variant_nonblock`) for the non-block consequent, where tsv re-collapses `if (a)‚èéexpr;` to `if (a) expr;`.

**Default / namespace import + export-all header comments**: the same preserve-in-place rule covers the remaining module-header shapes. In a **default** (`import /* c */ Foo from 'a'`) or **namespace** (`import /* c */ * as ns from 'a'`) import, tsv keeps each header comment where the user wrote it; Prettier keeps a comment already adjacent to the binding but relocates a comment between `import` and `type` to the binding side of `type` (`import type /* c */ Foo`). In an **export-all** (`export /* c */ * from 'a'`, including `export /* c */ type * from 'a'`) Prettier relocates _every_ header comment ‚Äî around `export`, `type`, and `*` ‚Äî to after `from`, before the source; tsv preserves them in place. A comment between `*` and `as` in a namespace binding (`import * /* c */ as ns`, `export * /* c */ as ns from 'a'`) is likewise preserved in place ‚Äî Prettier relocates it to after `as`, before the binding. Both positions are dual-stable in our formatter. Per the uniform module-header rule below, a line comment in **every** one of these gaps indents the continuation one level ‚Äî the keyword‚Üídefault/namespace binding, `type`‚Üídefault/namespace binding, `type`‚Üínamespace-`*`, export-all `export`/`type`‚Üí`*`, `*`‚Üí`from`, `*`‚Üí`as`, and `as`‚Üíbinding gaps alike. Where Prettier relocates (export-all, `*`‚Üí`as`) tsv is free; where Prettier keeps the comment in place and flat (keyword/`type`‚Üíbinding, `type`‚Üínamespace-`*`, `as`‚Üíbinding) tsv's indent is a deliberate indent-only divergence.

**Import/export binding-or-specifiers to `from`**: A comment in the gap between an import's binding/specifiers (or a re-export's specifiers) and the `from` keyword is preserved where the user placed it; Prettier's relocation depends on the binding shape. For a **default** or **namespace** binding (no braces) a same-line block comment stays in place in both formatters (`import Foo /* c */ from 'a'` ‚Äî dual-stable), but Prettier floats a line comment past the `;` to a statement-trailing position (`import Foo from 'a'; // c`, Prettier's statement-trailing float) while tsv keeps it before `from`, indenting the `from ‚Ä¶` continuation one level onto its own line. For **named specifiers** (`import { a } /* c */ from 'a'`, `export { a } /* c */ from 'a'`) Prettier relocates the comment _into_ the braces as the last specifier's trailing comment ‚Äî a block comment inline (`{ a /* c */ }`), a line comment expanding the braces multiline (`{\n\ta // c\n}`) ‚Äî while tsv keeps it after `}` with the braces inline (indenting `from ‚Ä¶` when a line comment forces the break). Both positions are dual-stable in our formatter. (Otherwise the comments are dropped entirely ‚Äî content loss.)

**Import attributes header comments**: A comment in an import's attributes header ‚Äî between the source and the `with` keyword (`import x from 'a' /* c */ with {‚Ä¶}`), or between `with` and the attributes `{` (`import x from 'a' with /* c */ {‚Ä¶}`) ‚Äî is preserved where the user placed it. Prettier keeps a source‚Üí`with` block comment in place (dual-stable), relocates a `with`‚Üí`{` block comment to before `with` (`import x from 'a' /* c */ with {‚Ä¶}`), and floats a `with`‚Üí`{` line comment past the `;` (`import x from 'a' with {‚Ä¶}; // c`, Prettier's statement-trailing float); for a source‚Üí`with` _line_ comment, Prettier collapses `with {‚Ä¶}` back onto the source line and floats the line comment past the `;` (`import b from './b' with {‚Ä¶}; // c`), while tsv keeps it before `with` ‚Äî see [with_keyword_comment_line](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/with_keyword_comment_line_prettier_divergence/). tsv keeps each comment where the user wrote it; when a line comment forces the `with`/`{‚Ä¶}` onto a new line, tsv indents that continuation one level. The attributes `}`‚Üí`;` block comment trails after the `;` in both formatters (the **Import source to `;`** entry below). (Otherwise the header comments are dropped entirely ‚Äî content loss.)

**Keyword ‚Üí specifier brace comments**: A comment between the `import`/`export` keyword and the named-specifier `{` (`import /* c */ { a }`, `export /* c */ { a }`) is preserved before the brace; Prettier relocates it _into_ the braces as the first specifier's leading comment ‚Äî a block comment inline (`import { /* c */ a }`), a line comment expanding the braces multiline. tsv keeps it where the user wrote it; a line comment forces `{` onto the next line, indenting the `{‚Ä¶}` continuation one level (the uniform module-header rule below). (The `import type ‚Ä¶ { a }` type‚Üí`{` gap and the empty-braces `import /* c */ {}` gap are preserved the same way; this is the non-type named-specifier case.) See [imports/keyword_brace_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/keyword_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/) and [exports/keyword_brace_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/exports/keyword_brace_comment_prettier_divergence/).

**Declaration- and module-header line-comment continuation indent**: A _line_ comment in a declaration- or module-header gap forces the following token onto a new line, and tsv indents that continuation one level ‚Äî a statement spanning lines reads as a continuation, not a second statement.

For **module headers** tsv applies this **uniformly to every gap, with no exceptions**: keyword‚Üí`type`, keyword/`type`‚Üídefault-binding, keyword/`type`‚Üínamespace-`*`, keyword/`type`‚Üí`{`, keyword/`type`‚Üíempty-`{}` (re-export _and_ no-`from`), bare keyword‚Üísource, export-all `export`/`type`‚Üí`*`, `*`‚Üí`from`, `*`‚Üí`as`, `as`‚Üíbinding, binding/specifiers‚Üí`from`, `from`‚Üísource, the `with`/attributes-`{` gaps, and `export`/`export default`‚Üídeclaration. Prettier's own handling varies per gap ‚Äî it relocates the comment (into the braces, after `from`/`as`/`;`), floats it past `;`, or keeps it in place and flat ‚Äî but tsv **always** indents. So where Prettier relocates, tsv's in-place indent is just one of two unrelated layouts; and where Prettier keeps the comment in place and flat (`as`‚Üíbinding, keyword/`type`‚Üídefault/namespace binding, `type`‚Üínamespace-`*`, bare/empty/export-all `from`‚Üísource, no-`from` empty `{}`, `export`‚Üídeclaration) tsv's indent is a deliberate indent-only divergence, chosen so every continuation reads alike.

For **declaration headers** the same rule covers the keyword‚Üíname gap of `function` (incl. `async function`, `function*`, and `declare function`), `class` (incl. `abstract class`), and `enum` (incl. `const enum`), plus the keyword‚Üídeclarator gap of `const`/`let`/`var`. Prettier keeps the comment in place and flat for the `function`/`class`/`enum` headers, so tsv's indent is an indent-only divergence there; for `const`/`let`/`var` Prettier **agrees** (it also indents the declarator), so there is no divergence ‚Äî a regular fixture.

The deliberate exclusions are constructs where the following token isn't part of the same declaration: **ASI statement keywords** (`return`, `throw`, `break`, `continue`, `yield`) ‚Äî a newline after them triggers automatic semicolon insertion, so `return // c‚èéexpr` is two statements, not a continuation; the **contextual declaration keywords** (`type`/`interface`/`namespace`/`module`/`declare`), whose line forms never form a single declaration ‚Äî the keyword requires its following token on the **same line** (tsc's `isDeclaration`: `nextTokenIsIdentifierOnSameLine`, and the ASI modifier rule for `declare`), so a line break demotes the keyword to a plain identifier. `interface`/`namespace`/`module`‚Üíname then become unparseable (`interface // c‚èéI {}` is rejected); `type`‚Üíname and `declare`‚Üíkeyword **ASI-split** into two statements (`type;` then `T = ‚Ä¶`; `declare;` then `const x = ‚Ä¶`). tsv's parser conforms here ‚Äî see [contextual_keywords/declaration_keyword_own_line](../tests/fixtures/typescript/syntax/contextual_keywords/declaration_keyword_own_line/); and **function/class expressions** (`const a = function // c‚èéf() {}`), which are not declaration headers and stay flat in both formatters. Block comments and the no-comment case are byte-identical in every in-scope gap. (The `export`-prefixed forms ‚Äî `export interface // c‚èéI` etc. ‚Äî are out of scope: after `export` the parser is committed to a declaration, where tsc does not apply the same-line gate, so tsv's acceptance there may be spec-correct; acorn-typescript rejects them, but that is a separate acorn-vs-tsc question.)

**Keyword-paren comments**: `if/* c */(a)` ‚Üí Prettier absorbs comments between keywords and `(` into the condition parens. Applies to `if`, `while`, `for`, `switch`, `catch`, `do...while`. tsv preserves the comment between keyword and paren: `if /* c */ (a)`. For `for await`, comments in either gap are preserved: `for /* a */ await /* b */ (x of y)` ‚Üí prettier absorbs both into parens. The only divergence is the comment position ‚Äî the loop body layout still matches Prettier regardless: an empty body attaches as `for /* k */ (a; b; c);` (no space before `;`), a block body hugs `) {`, and a non-block body stays inline when the header fits ([keyword_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/for/keyword_comment_prettier_divergence/)). Both positions are dual-stable in our formatter.

**Condition-absorbed comments**: `switch(x)/* c */{}` ‚Üí Prettier absorbs comments between `)` and `{` into the condition parens: `switch (x /* c */) {}`. Similarly, `catch/* c */(e)` ‚Üí `catch (/* c */ e)`. tsv preserves position: `switch (x) /* c */ {}`, `catch /* c */ (e)`. Both positions are dual-stable in our formatter.

**Type alias head to `=`**: `type A<X>\n// c\n= B | C` ‚Üí Prettier relocates a line comment between a type alias head (name + optional type parameters) and `=` to after `=` (`type A<X> =\n// c\nB | C`). tsv preserves it before `=`, keeping the comment's association with the declaration head rather than the value. (With type parameters present, the comment is otherwise easily dropped entirely ‚Äî content loss.) A single-line block comment before `=` stays inline in both formatters (`type A<X> /* c */ = B | C`), so it is not a divergence ‚Äî only a line comment forces the value to the next line, and the two formatters disagree on which side of `=` it lands. Both positions are dual-stable in our formatter. When the value is a **break-forced non-hugging union** (broken by print width or by interleaved member comments), tsv drops `=` onto its own line below the comment and hangs the union members at the **`=`'s indent level** ‚Äî the same level the author wrote and byte-identical to Prettier's union block, just with `=` lifted above it rather than the members one level deeper ([type_alias_line_pre_equals_break](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/type_alias_line_pre_equals_break_prettier_divergence/)). Conditional / intersection / object / short-union values hug `= ` and are unaffected; only the non-hugging union, whose broken form leads every member with `|` on its own line, drops `=` alone.

**Type parameter keyword to value (own-line)**: an own-line line comment between a type parameter's `extends`/`=` keyword and its constraint/default value (`U =\n// c\nV`, `T extends\n// c\nA`) is kept on its own line in the indented value block; Prettier pulls the first leading comment up onto the keyword line (`U = // c\n\tV`) and is **non-idempotent** doing so (its first pass leaves the value at the param indent, a second pass adds the extra indent). tsv stays idempotent and preserves the author's own-line placement. A comment that is **already** on the keyword line (`R extends A | B | void = // c\n‚Ä¶`): tsv emits it inline via `line_suffix` (zero width), so a long trailing comment never forces a preceding constraint union to break. Prettier instead counts the trailing comment toward the line width and breaks after `extends` (`R extends\n\tA | B | void = // c\n‚Ä¶`), so this is a divergence ([type_param_keyword_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/type_param_keyword_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)); the own-line first-comment case diverges separately (below). (Emitting the same-line comment as plain text would force-break the constraint union by its width ‚Äî content added ‚Äî and merge two line comments onto one line ‚Äî boundary loss; the `line_suffix` rendering avoids both.) See [type_param_keyword_own_line_comment_prettier_divergence](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/comments/type_param_keyword_own_line_comment_prettier_divergence/).

**Function parameter default to value**: a line comment after a parameter's `=` default, before the value (`function fn(p = // c\n\tv) {}`), is kept after `=` with the value on the next line; Prettier floats it out to trail the whole parameter, after the value (`function fn(\n\tp = v // c\n) {}`). tsv keeps the comment associated with the default rather than floating it past the value. The parameter's type-annotation union stays inline in both (the trailing comment is zero-width). Applies to function, arrow, and method parameters; a same-line block comment (`p = /* c */ v`) stays inline in both formatters and is not a divergence. See [param_default_line_comment_prettier_divergence](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/function/param_default_line_comment_prettier_divergence/).

**Name/key to default `=`** (the *before*-`=` counterpart): a line comment between a binding name/key and its `=` default (`p // c\n= v`), at a parameter default and every destructuring default ‚Äî object shorthand (`{ a // c\n= 1 }`), array element (`[b // c\n= 1]`), and function-param destructure (`fn({ c // c\n= 1 })`) ‚Äî is kept trailing the name with `= value` broken to the next line; the pattern expands to accommodate it. Prettier instead relocates the comment to trail the whole binding after the value (`{ a = 1 // c }`, expanded). tsv keeps the comment where the author wrote it (between name and `=`); emitting it inline would let the `//` swallow the `=` and default value (a non-idempotent content loss). A same-line block comment (`{ a /* c */ = 1 }`) stays inline in both formatters and is not a divergence (see the block-comment sibling [default_equals_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/destructuring/default_equals_comment/)). See [default_equals_line_comment_prettier_divergence](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/destructuring/default_equals_line_comment_prettier_divergence/).

**`as`/`satisfies` cast keyword to type**: a line comment after the cast keyword, before the type (`x as // c\n\tA`), is kept after the keyword with the type on the next line; Prettier floats it out past the whole expression to a statement-trailing position (`x as A; // c`). tsv keeps the comment associated with the cast, on the keyword line via `line_suffix` with the type indented; emitting it inline instead would **swallow the cast type** (`x as // c A` ‚Äî a non-idempotent content loss). A same-line block comment (`x as /* c */ A`) stays inline in both formatters and is not a divergence. See [as_satisfies_value_line_comment_prettier_divergence](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_satisfies_value_line_comment_prettier_divergence/). A **block** comment in the same gap collapses to the inline form (`x as /* c */ A`) ‚Äî whether authored glued, trailing the keyword, or on its own line (`x as‚èé/* c */‚èéA`). tsv keeps it after the keyword, associated with the cast type; Prettier collapses too but *relocates* the comment _before_ the keyword (`x /* c */ as A`). The block counterpart of the line case above ‚Äî see the keyword‚Üívalue block-comment collapse rule below and [as_satisfies_value_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/as_satisfies_value_own_line_block_comment_prettier_divergence/).

**Binary operand to operator line comment**: a line comment after a binary chain's left operand, before the operator (`1 // c\n+ 2`), is kept trailing the operand where the author wrote it, and the operator drops to the next line glued to its right operand (`1 // c\n+ 2`); Prettier relocates the comment _past_ the operator, keeping the operator trailing the left operand (`1 + // c\n2`). tsv preserves the comment's association with the left operand ([Comment Position Philosophy](#comment-position-philosophy) Principles 1 and 2). Emitting it inline instead would run to end-of-line and **swallow the operator and right operand** (`1 // c + 2` ‚Äî `+ 2` absorbed into the comment, a non-idempotent content loss). The operator hugs its right operand rather than over-breaking onto a line of its own (`1 // c\n+\n2`); in a longer chain each boundary is independent, so an uncommented gap keeps the normal break-after-operator (`aa &&\nbb // c\n&& cc`). Covers arithmetic, logical, and the keyword-binary operators (`in`, `instanceof`) ‚Äî all `BinaryExpression` through the one binary-chain printer (`build_binary_chain_parts`, `operators.rs`). A same-line block comment (`1 /* c */ + 2`) stays inline in both formatters and is not a divergence. See [operand_operator_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/binary/operand_operator_line_comment_prettier_divergence/).

**Call open paren `(` trailing**: `fn( // c` / `fn( /* c */` (a comment on the same line as a call's opening `(`) ‚Üí Prettier relocates it to its own line as the first argument's leading comment (`fn(\n\t// c\n\t‚Ä¶)`). tsv keeps it trailing the `(` (`fn( // c\n\t‚Ä¶)`), treating the author's placement after `(` as a trailing comment on that line. This applies only when the call expands (a line comment after `(`, or own-line content among the args); a block comment that hugs the arg in a call that stays inline (`fn(/* c */ a)`) is unchanged and matches Prettier. When the author instead writes the comment on its own line, both formatters keep it there ‚Äî the two positions are dual-stable. Applies to simple-callee calls (`call_formatting.rs`), member-chain calls (`chain_args.rs`), and `new` expressions (`new_expression.rs`). For chains, a block comment trailing `(` plus an own-line leading comment keep source order (the naive handling reverses them). For `new`, a line comment trailing `(` (`new Foo( // c\n\ta)`) is preserved rather than dropped entirely (content loss); prettier relocates it (line or block) to its own line inside the parens as the first argument's leading comment (`new Foo(\n\t// c\n\ta)`), the same as the simple-callee and member-chain forms.

**Object/array/block open-delimiter trailing**: the same position-preservation rule as the call `(` case, generalized to the other opening delimiters. A comment on the same line as an object literal's `{` (`const o = { // c`), an array literal's `[` (`const a = [ // c`), a block body's `{` (`function f() { // c`, plain `{ // c`, arrow `=> { // c`), a type-parameter list's `<` (`function f< // c`, also classes/interfaces/type aliases/arrows), a function/constructor-type parameter list's `(` (`type Fn = ( // c`, `new ( // c`), a **value-level function-definition** parameter list's `(` (`function fn( // c`, `function ( // c`, `( // c ) => ‚Ä¶`, and class method / constructor / setter ‚Äî [open_paren_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/declarations/function/open_paren_line_comment_prettier_divergence/), [method_open_paren_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/statements/class/method_open_paren_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)), an object/array destructuring pattern's `{`/`[` (`const { // c } = o`, `const [ // c ] = a`), a `namespace`/`module` body's `{` (`namespace N { // c`, `module M { // c`), a class/interface/enum body's `{` (`class C { // c`, `interface I { // c`, `enum E { // c`), a type literal's `{` (`type T = { // c`), an import/export specifier list's `{` (`import { // c`, `export { // c`), a tuple type's `[` (`type T = [ // c`), an index signature's `[` (`[ // c\n\tk: V]`), a computed property/member key's `[` (`{ [ // c\n\tfoo]: 1 }`, also class members, destructuring, and interface/type-literal members ‚Äî [computed_key_glued_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/objects/computed_key_glued_block_comment_prettier_divergence/), which also pins prettier hoisting an in-bracket block comment out to the member's line), a mapped-type key's `[` (`{ [ // c\n\tK in keyof T]: V }` ‚Äî prettier drops it to its own line ‚Äî [mapped_key_glued_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/types/mapped_key_glued_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)), a computed member-access index's `[` (element access, `arr[ // c\n\ti]`, including optional `?.[` ‚Äî prettier relocates it to trail the object), an angle-bracket type assertion's `<` (`const x = < // c\n\tT>y` ‚Äî [angle_glued_block_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/expressions/type_assertion/angle_glued_block_comment_prettier_divergence/)), or a multi-argument type-argument list's `<` (`Map< // c`) is kept on the delimiter line; Prettier relocates it to its own line as the leading comment of the first element/property/statement/parameter/member/specifier/argument (for a computed key prettier instead relocates it out to the **member's** own leading line, or ‚Äî class members ‚Äî leaves it glued flush to the key). This applies only to a **line** comment (or a block comment that co-occurs with one) when the construct expands; an inline block comment that hugs content (`{ /* c */ a: 1 }`, `[/* c */ x]`, `<T /* c */>`, `(/* c */ p)`) and an own-line block comment (which both formatters keep on its own line) are unchanged and match Prettier. (An empty brace body whose sole content is that inline block comment, `{ /* c */ }`, likewise hugs rather than relocating ‚Äî but tsv keeps its bracket spacing where Prettier 3.9.5 tightens it to `{/* c */}`, a separate divergence: see the ¬ßEmpty-object comment bracket spacing entry above.) When the author instead writes the comment on its own line, both formatters keep it there ‚Äî dual-stable. Object literals are handled in `objects.rs`, arrays in `arrays.rs`, block bodies in the shared block-printing path (`expressions/blocks.rs`), type-parameter declarations in `types/type_params.rs` (covering function/class/interface/type-alias/arrow), function/constructor types in `types/function_types.rs`, value-level function-definition parameter lists (function declarations/expressions, arrows, class methods, constructors, setters, and Svelte `{#snippet}` params) in `build_params_doc_with_comments` (`expressions/functions.rs`, via the same `delimiter_line_comment_prefix` helper as the signature path), object/array destructuring patterns in `expressions/patterns.rs`, `namespace`/`module` bodies in the shared statement-list walk (`statements/type_declarations.rs`, reusing `build_statement_list_docs_into`), class/interface/enum bodies in their member loops (`build_class_body_doc` in `statements/class.rs`; `build_type_elements_doc` and `build_enum_declaration_doc` in `statements/type_declarations.rs`), type literals in the multiline member path (`build_type_literal_doc_inner` ‚Üí `build_multiline_member_prefix_doc`, `types/type_literal.rs`), import/export specifier lists in the shared multiline comma-list builder (`build_hardline_comma_list`, `statements/modules/specifier_list.rs`; the `with {‚Ä¶}` import-attribute brace passes its first attribute's start through the same builder ‚Äî [with_open_brace_line_comment](../tests/fixtures/typescript/modules/imports/with_open_brace_line_comment_prettier_divergence/)), tuple types in their multiline element path (`build_tuple_type_doc_with_line_comments`, `types/composite.rs`, using `build_leading_comments_multiline` for the first element), index signatures in `build_index_signature_member_doc` (`types/type_members.rs`), computed property/member keys in `build_computed_key_bracket_doc` (`expressions/objects.rs`, its breaking path ‚Äî a computed key never breaks on width, so a line comment in either in-bracket gap, `[`‚Üíkey (this case) or key‚Üí`]` (the [close-bracket sibling](#comment-relocation)), is the only trigger;
